3321/*-



3322 * The generated code includes comments that allow you to trace directly



3323 * back to the appropriate location in the model.  The basic format



3324 * is <system>/block_name, where system is the system number (uniquely



3325 * assigned by Simulink) and block_name is the name of the block.



3326 *



3327 * Use the MATLAB hilite_system command to trace the generated code back



3328 * to the model.  For example,



3329 *



3330 * hilite_system('<S3>')    - opens system 3



3331 * hilite_system('<S3>/Kp') - opens and selects block Kp which resides in S3



3332 *
